  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_da447d6b-8f88-46f0-9042-5ecbf2ca5e87'
      });

  <span id="freeText12331195670801019903" style="display:none"><i>alternate cover edition of <b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/49226269" rel="nofollow noopener">ISBN 9781416509882</a></b></i><br /><br />In this next installment in the <i>Immortals After Dark Series</i>, <i>USA Today</i> Bestselling author Kresley Cole delivers a scorching tale about a forbidding vampire who lives in the shadows and the beautiful assassin who hunts him there. <br /><br /><b>A vampire soldier weary of life...</b><br /><br />Centuries ago, Sebastian Wroth was turned into a vampire—a nightmare in his mind—against his will. Burdened with hatred and alone for ages, he sees little reason to live. Until an exquisite, fey creature comes to kill him, inadvertently saving him instead.<br /><br /><b>A valkyrie assassin dispatched to destroy him...</b><br /><br />When Kaderin the Cold Hearted lost her two beloved sisters to a vampire attack long ago, a benevolent force deadened her sorrow—accidentally extinguishing all of her emotions. Yet whenever she encounters Sebastian, her feelings—particularly lust—emerge multiplied. For the first time, she's unable to complete a kill.<br /><br /><b>Competitors in a legendary hunt...</b><br /><br />The prize of the month-long contest is powerful enough to change history, and Kaderin will do anything to win it for her sisters. Wanting only to win her, forever, Sebastian competes as well, taking every opportunity—as they travel to ancient tombs and through catacombs, seeking relics around the world—to use her new feelings to seduce her. But when forced to choose between the vampire she's falling for and reuniting her family, how can Kaderin live without either?</span>

          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: 6000})});
        }
      });

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');

        $('edition_7003386').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('edition_7003386').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;

            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });

<div class='communityQuestion'>
<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/836961-is-this-plot-in-here-the-same-as-a-hunger">Is this plot in here the same as A Hunger like No Other and Wicked Deeds on a Winter&#39;s night? I just got done reading both of those and the relationship unfolded in the exact same way with everyone having the same personality and using the same phrases. I can&#39;t take any more of the arguing and repeated failed attempts at the love scenes because of it.</a>
</div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1587117545" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11432145969589563133">Now that I've picked this series up again, I can't put it down! I'm loving this supernatural world that Kresley Cole created. Slowly but surely, I'm figuring out these mystical beings and beginning to connect the dots between their stories. The audiobook narration continues to be fantastic as well.<br/><br/>Like the second book in the series, 'No Rest For The Wicked' centers on the forbidden romance between a Valkyrie and a vampire. This time around, it is Kaderin the cold-hearted and Sebastian that end u</span>
  <span id="freeText11432145969589563133" style="display:none">Now that I've picked this series up again, I can't put it down! I'm loving this supernatural world that Kresley Cole created. Slowly but surely, I'm figuring out these mystical beings and beginning to connect the dots between their stories. The audiobook narration continues to be fantastic as well.<br /><br />Like the second book in the series, 'No Rest For The Wicked' centers on the forbidden romance between a Valkyrie and a vampire. This time around, it is Kaderin the cold-hearted and Sebastian that end up being "mated". <br /><br />Once again, we're gifted with an extremely sexy alpha-male and a less than enthused "bride". Although there were many similarities to this book's predecessor, 'The Warlord Wants Forever', I found this book to be entertaining and sexy. You just can't get too much of a good thing! Ms. Cole has figured out a formula that works for her series and I'm completely enthralled.<br /><br />If you haven't read this series, I highly recommend it. I'm listening to the fourth book now and I continue to be captivated by this story. The characters are well developed and compelling. The chemistry is off the charts. I have no complaints.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11432145969589563133" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_149807627" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/149807627" />
    <a title="Kat Kennedy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3270188-kat-kennedy"><img alt="Kat Kennedy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1537750381p2/3270188.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/149807627?book_show_action=true">Feb 22, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kat Kennedy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kat Kennedy" href="/user/show/3270188-kat-kennedy">Kat Kennedy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=kat-s-book-reviews">kat-s-book-reviews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=romance-romance-romance">romance-romance-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer149807627" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3456511975523392208">I have a scientific curiosity about romance readers. I want to probe them like rats in a cage.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380346013i/700509._SX540_.jpg' alt='probe' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>Don't worry, I'll be gentle... if you want me to.</i><br/><br/>What do they like about these novels? What characteristics appeal to them? What is the common denominator in a successful romance novel? Can I boil it down and make a formula.<br/><br/>Quality of foreplay X chemistry / sexual tension over time (grading scale being >50 for way too early, =80 for perfection and around 100 for aggravating over-tension, otherwise known</span>
  <span id="freeText3456511975523392208" style="display:none">I have a scientific curiosity about romance readers. I want to probe them like rats in a cage.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380346013i/700509._SX540_.jpg" alt="probe" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Don't worry, I'll be gentle... if you want me to.</i><br><br>What do they like about these novels? What characteristics appeal to them? What is the common denominator in a successful romance novel? Can I boil it down and make a formula.<br><br>Quality of foreplay X chemistry / sexual tension over time (grading scale being &gt;50 for way too early, =80 for perfection and around 100 for aggravating over-tension, otherwise known and "Oh, FFS! Just do it already!")<br><br>But then you'd have to add in other complex formulas for likability of both the male and female protagonists (completely separate formulas), balancing action and ridiculously contrived plots with heaving bosoms. When I began on my complex mathematical studies, I had no ideas it would be so difficult to boil down!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380346013i/700510._SX540_.jpg" alt="sex" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>You mean there's more to it than this?</i><br><br>I enjoyed this novel because it confounded quite a few of my formulas. Also, it may as well be retitled Kat and Mr Kennedy if They Lived in Paranormal Romance World. <br><br>Kaderine is cold and emotionless (see where the similarities begin?) until she meets Sebastian who despises his life as a vampire. Unable to kill him, she runs and he chases her.<br><br>Now, what COULD have progressed was a tale of an alpha male chasing down his woman until she finally relented, realized how much she wanted his gorgeous body (and all appendages) and finally succumbed to her Stockholm Syndrome.<br><br>What progressed was Kaderine spending 95% of this novel kicking ass and not ONCE being whiny or pathetic. What progressed was Sebastian discovering that he could not control, dominate or cage Kaderine because she would never love him that way. What progressed was him realizing he wanted to help her achieve her dream because he cared about her and loved her EXACTLY the way she was without even trying to take her away from her family, her life or her passions.<br><br>Finally.<br><br>A relationship dynamic that DOESN'T make me feel slightly queasy. <br><br>This novel was pretty good. It almost manages to wipe away the bitter memories of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/14384.A_Hunger_Like_No_Other__Immortals_After_Dark___2_" title="A Hunger Like No Other (Immortals After Dark, #2) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">A Hunger Like No Other</a> and in my opinion, the characters, action and story are infinitely better.<br><br>Cole has JUST convinced me to keep reading. If it hadn't been for her loyal fans then I would have ditched her halfway through the first book. She should pay them money. Lots and lots of money.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380346013i/700511.jpg" alt="sexy" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Like, enough to buy each of them one of these.</i><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="3456511975523392208" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Blacky *Romance Addict*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Blacky *Romance Addict*" href="/user/show/8310179-blacky-romance-addict">Blacky *Romance Addict*</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer344861739" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12205881911455464398"><b><br/>This book has the most realistic insta-love in a PNR that I've ever read!<br/><br/><a target='_blank' href='https://imageshack.com/i/n1522dg' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394713765ra/8894412.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/><br/><br/>Seriously, I am surprised how the author did it and it made me bump it up a star. I just couldn't believe it!</b><br/><br/><a target='_blank' href='https://imageshack.com/i/go71118612g' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394713765ra/8894413.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/><br/>I know comparing books isn't the thing, especially in reviews but I just have to explain why this shocked me so :D<br/>I'm currently reading another paranormal series that has to do with vampires, and I just couldn't NOT compare these two, especially because this one has a vampire as male lead too.<br/><br/>Anyway, you know how</span>
  <span id="freeText12205881911455464398" style="display:none"><b><br>This book has the most realistic insta-love in a PNR that I've ever read!<br><br><a target="_blank" href="https://imageshack.com/i/n1522dg" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394713765ra/8894412.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><br>Seriously, I am surprised how the author did it and it made me bump it up a star. I just couldn't believe it!</b><br><br><a target="_blank" href="https://imageshack.com/i/go71118612g" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394713765ra/8894413.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>I know comparing books isn't the thing, especially in reviews but I just have to explain why this shocked me so :D<br>I'm currently reading another paranormal series that has to do with vampires, and I just couldn't NOT compare these two, especially because this one has a vampire as male lead too.<br><br>Anyway, you know how it is in most PNR books, 2/3 of the time we get the insta-love and the "MINE" thing, and I'm OK with that because it's just the way it goes, though in some it's made more realistic than others.<br><br>Like the last book I've read had a vampire and a human falling in love after 4 days of knowing each other and maybe having 3 conversations all-together. And I mean falling in uber LOVE, for forever, where they have so many strong feelings for one another. After like 4 days. And at the end something happens that separates them and the dude wonders "how come she doesn't know me better than that, I thought she loved me"? Dude, YOU ONLY KNEW EACH OTHER FOR 4 F*CKING DAYS!!!!!!!!<br><br><a target="_blank" href="https://imageshack.com/i/nl1253g" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394713765ra/8894414.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Now this book...<br><br><b>Kresley Cole did it right. Boy, did she do it right!<br><br>Insta-love writers, take a hint from THIS!!!!!!!!!</b><br><br><br><br>There is insta-something in this book, right at the start of it, the two protagonists realise they are "mates" in the first scene of the book :DDDDD<br>BUT!<br>Kaderin hates vampires and wants nothing to do with Sebastian, nd the poor dude spends almost the entire book convincing her he is different and that they are meant to be together.<br><br>This isn't what was different here, actually this is pretty much how every PNR goes LOL<br><br><br><b>THIS is what surprised me:<br><br>*quote from Sebastian*<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>"Myst goes on the computer each day and checks the results. She has a half-sister in the competition. Is she your Bride?"<br>"Yes," he admitted. "Kaderin."<br>"Myst has told me Kaderin is--how did she put it?--'gorgeous to a near freakish degree.' And a stalwart fighter." His tone hopeful, Nikolai asked, "Do you love her?"<br>"No. But I recognize that she is mine. And that I am meant to protect her."<br>"It's enough. More will come with time," Nikolai said.<br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>This is the most realistic view on the "mine" thing. He recognises she is his, but there isn't any real love yet because they simply don't know each other. And I just love the author for doing this, I really do.<br><br><br><br>*quote from Kaderin*<br><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">["Look, Sebastian, am I attracted to you? Yep, you got me. I'm not going to lie. Last night was... enjoyable. I'm glad it happened. But that doesn't mean that it will happen again. Much less that I will wed you."<br>"What could make it so that you would?"<br>"My absolute belief that I would want to spend eternity with you. Immortals really have to be careful with this, you understand, and you and I have never even had a civil conversation before today. And honestly, I don't trust you, and I can't turn off a lifetime of beliefs in the course of two weeks." <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><a target="_blank" href="https://imageshack.com/i/12179tg" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394713765ra/8894415.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><br>I was speechless after this, mainly because it was in the second half of the book and she still thought this, so yeah, I gotta say I just love how it was done!<br><br><br>Kresley Cole, you rock!!!!!</b><br><br><br><br>Anyway, about the rest of the book ehehehhehehehheheh<br><br><b>I listened to the audiobook</b> here and the narrator is simply amazing (&lt;3 &lt;3 &lt;3 &lt;3 &lt;3), though Sebastian has a sort of Russian accent, but not quite, something similar as me trying to speak English ahahhahahahah so I sympathize with the guy :D<br><br><br><b>I like how the story here is really weird and different</b>, there isn't an uber PNR bad guy or some evil thing or a war or i don't know what that makes the suspense, the games in which Kaderin competes are the center of it and they were awesome! one scene in particular was sooooo horrible and scary and written so well though I kinda hate it cause it was so scary ahahhahahahahahah (for those of you who've read this, it's the shark scene :SSSS).<br><br><br><b>I actually meant to give this 4 stars, but as the book went on, it got better, then much better, then great, then amazing, then freaking awesome, so you see why I had to bump it up :D<br><br><br>So there, a huge rec from me, for those of you who are sick of the classic insta-love in PNR, you won't find it here ;))))</b><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1269285103" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2889210090181637075"><b>Spoilers</b><br/><br/>So Good..... All I can say about this series so far is WOW!!!!!!!!! I am so loving this series.<br/><br/>Kaderin the Cold Hearted is a Kickass Warrior Valkyrie who hates vampires because she had mercy on a vampire and he turned around and killer her two sisters. <span id="freeTextContainer2196136866086705000"><b>
  <blockquote>“And now, for the first time in three hundred hellish years, Sebastian desperately wanted to live.” </blockquote>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1482594232i/21531492._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Sebastian Wroth is my favorite type of hero. He's persistent, gentle, adamant and freaking hot ! I fell in love with this book since the first chapter. Kresley Cole outlined No Rest for the Wicked very well because she didn't left any details out. The beginning of it and the ending were powerful, I felt emotions through the book even when I didn't read it, it was still there. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1482594232ra/21531493.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>

  <blockquote>“And now, for the first time in three hundred hellish years, Sebastian desperately wanted to live.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1482594232i/21531492._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sebastian Wroth is my favorite type of hero. He's persistent, gentle, adamant and freaking hot ! I fell in love with this book since the first chapter. Kresley Cole outlined No Rest for the Wicked very well because she didn't left any details out. The beginning of it and the ending were powerful, I felt emotions through the book even when I didn't read it, it was still there. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1482594232ra/21531493.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“They desecrate Riora’s sacred temple! She will be enraged.”<br>“Oh, gods, look at the marble. We are all beyond doomed.”<br>“Somebody put a plant in front of it!” </blockquote>
</b><br><br>Apart from Sebastian's persistent characteristic, he's the one moving the story forward and putting power in each pace of the story. While I hated Kaderin for being an idiot sometimes, her character still moved me along with Sebastian's without any concerns. Their coupling is so perfect I didn't feel anything out of place.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“I'd wear his corsage to an orgy, any day!”</blockquote>
</b> <br><br>To be honest, this book was enjoyable and that unexpected twist almost tore me apart. I loved every minute of reading it. It thrilled me until I couldn't sit still for the next round of gutwrenching action scenes. It's worth the re-reading !<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1482594233ra/21531494.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://goo.gl/Wx2hBE">https://goo.gl/Wx2hBE</a></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2002749998" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer5131683314886461643"><b>Sebastian Wroth (Vampire) & Kaderin the Cold Hearted (Valkyrie)</b><br/><br/>Sebastian Wroth never wanted to become a vampire. <br/>That September of 1709, he only wished to die. Everything he loved was lost, died, taken away from him. Sebastian was a man of honor. Better to have a honorable death, than becoming a bloodthirsty Vampiir. His brother Nikolai who suddenly appeared had other plans.<br/><br/><i>“I will not have this for me,” Sebastian said. “I do not want it.”<br/>“You must, brother,” Nikolai murmured. Were his eerie eye</i></span>
  <span id="freeText5131683314886461643" style="display:none"><b>Sebastian Wroth (Vampire) &amp; Kaderin the Cold Hearted (Valkyrie)</b><br /><br />Sebastian Wroth never wanted to become a vampire. <br />That September of 1709, he only wished to die. Everything he loved was lost, died, taken away from him. Sebastian was a man of honor. Better to have a honorable death, than becoming a bloodthirsty Vampiir. His brother Nikolai who suddenly appeared had other plans.<br /><br /><i>“I will not have this for me,” Sebastian said. “I do not want it.”<br />“You must, brother,” Nikolai murmured. Were his eerie eyes glinting? “Otherwise you die tonight.”</i><br /><br />Nowadays, Sebastian still has not forgiven his brother. He still lives at his castle in Esthonia, all alone, hating himself and wishing to die. He never understood what being a vampire means. He never learned that the Earth is full of other supernatural immortals beings as well. He only wishes that someone kills him. <br /><br />And then Kaderin, the valkirie appears ready to kill him. And they both realize that Kaderin is his bride. <br />Naturally, Sebastian has just discovered an important reason for him to live. He has to be with Kaderin, to protect her, to cherish her, to spoil her, to love her forever. <br /><br />Yes, Kaderin is not happy. She hates vampires. They killed her sisters a few centuries ago. She wants to destroy all of them. She does not feel anything. No time for romance – especially with the enemy.<br /><br />But they both, although not very experienced, cannot stop the attraction<br /><br /><i>“You are unused to this.” He traced across the room and stood, arms out, a hand on each side of the doorway. “As am I. We will find our way with this together. But you are my Bride.”<br />She closed her eyes, struggling for calm. “You’re not my husband. And never will be.”<br />“This can’t be random, Kaderin.”</i><br /><br />Previously secluded Sebastian will try to learn everything he can about this new century, about the technology and the manners; while at the same time he will try to learn everything about the Lore and its creatures. <br />He never really tried to fit in before, but now he really wants to be worthy for his bride.<br /><br />Kaderin will try to ignore Sebastian (unsuccessfully) and she will enter the Hie competition -where the majority of the Lore factions are represented - to win the ultimate price in order to gain back her lost happiness all these centuries. <br /><br />Sebastian will enter as well and he is determined to help Kaderin – even if she does not wish his help.<br /><br />Sebastian’s brother, Nikolai, is also determined to help Sebastian – even if he does not wish his help. <br />Nikolai loves his brother and he understands what it means to have a Valkyrie as a bride.<br /><br />Gradually Sebastian and Kaderin will fall in love and their mating will be explosive.<br /><br />Super awesome out of this world addition to the series. I am sure all PNR fans cry with joy every time they read this book :)</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/316651466?book_show_action=true">Apr 21, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristen" href="/user/show/5477946-kristen">Kristen</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>

      Karla
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=5-star">5-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=favorite-books">favorite-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=action-packed">action-packed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=great-ending">great-ending</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=medium-steam">medium-steam</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=fabulous-characters">fabulous-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=fabulous-heroine">fabulous-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=feel-good-read">feel-good-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=humorous">humorous</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer316651466" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15612798917543675581"><b>Huge 5 stars</b><br/><br/>I had a blast reading this story! I'm also sure it will come as no surprise to those who've followed my status updates that I freaking LOVED this book!<br/><br/>Right from the start, <i>No Rest for the Wicked</i> had me captivated and giddy. I couldn't stop myself from giggling, laughing, clapping, and squealing with delight while I cheering the characters on in their quest to win the Talisman's Hie, the immortals' version of the TV show the Amazing Race. I also found myself eager for the love story </span>
  <span id="freeText15612798917543675581" style="display:none"><b>Huge 5 stars</b><br /><br />I had a blast reading this story! I'm also sure it will come as no surprise to those who've followed my status updates that I freaking LOVED this book!<br /><br />Right from the start, <i>No Rest for the Wicked</i> had me captivated and giddy. I couldn't stop myself from giggling, laughing, clapping, and squealing with delight while I cheering the characters on in their quest to win the Talisman's Hie, the immortals' version of the TV show the Amazing Race. I also found myself eager for the love story to be resolved, as I felt the hero truly deserved his HEA. <br /><br />About the hero... boy, did I fall-head-over-heels for Sebastian. He's everything a true hero should be: honorable, courageous, fierce, loyal, tender, aggressive, sexy, thoughtful and protective. He definitely earn a spot among my all-time favorite heroes. As for the heroine, Kaderin the Coldhearted, I wasn't her biggest fan for a good portion of this book. She was every bit as "coldhearted" as her name implies. However, once she gained her emotions back, realized what a good man (vampire) Sebastian was, and proved she was worthy of him, I fell in love with her, too. Sebastian and Kaderin made a great couple and I hope to get more of them in future books. <br /><br /><i>No Rest for the Wicked</i> was an absolutely delightful read. I ended this book with a huge smile on my face. I honestly can't remember the last time I had so much fun reading a book! <br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15612798917543675581" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_300376256" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/300376256" />
    <a title="Exina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5309539-exina"><img alt="Exina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1580809437p2/5309539.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/300376256?book_show_action=true">Mar 25, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Exina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Exina" href="/user/show/5309539-exina">Exina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=4-star-still-favorites">4-star-still-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=great-characterization">great-characterization</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=action-and-thrill">action-and-thrill</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=alpha-males">alpha-males</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=badass-heroine">badass-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=multi-paranormal-species">multi-paranormal-species</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=complex-characters">complex-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=m-f">m-f</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=series">series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer300376256" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13047546279006493261"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"If you love something, you protect it ruthlessly. No matter what occurs."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>This series is getting better and better. The 3rd book in the 'Immortals After Dark' series by Kresley Cole is full of extreme ideas, a fast-paced plot, exquisite characters and brilliant humor.<br/><br/>The events revolve around <b>the Talisman’s Hie,</b> a contest for immortals, where the ultimate price is unimaginably precious, and the setting is more than adventurous. This savage, bloody competition gives another peek into </span>
  <span id="freeText13047546279006493261" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"If you love something, you protect it ruthlessly. No matter what occurs."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>This series is getting better and better. The 3rd book in the 'Immortals After Dark' series by Kresley Cole is full of extreme ideas, a fast-paced plot, exquisite characters and brilliant humor.<br><br>The events revolve around <b>the Talisman’s Hie,</b> a contest for immortals, where the ultimate price is unimaginably precious, and the setting is more than adventurous. This savage, bloody competition gives another peek into the fabulous world Kresley Cole created. It is an amazing alternative reality, with fascinating characters, and sometimes I just feel I want to be a part of it myself so bad.<br><br><b>Sebastian and Kaderin’s first scene proves how important and overpowering fate is in this world.</b><br>Their relationship, reactions and feelings for each other are expressed on a very special level. They are hundreds or thousands of years-old immortals. They can’t behave like humans, their relationship can’t be standard. Their problems and mentality are strongly different than the problems of contemporary romance characters. They are driven by fate, instincts and power. I love these powerful and limitless strong emotions.<br><br><b>Sebastian</b> is irresistible, ingenious, determined. He is always honest and loyal.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469620714i/19837675._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“A hint, Sebastian? I you’re courting a woman, you could pause a nanosecond before declaring that you don’t love her. Maybe act as though you’d considered the possibility. Or you could lie. Or you could gloss over it by predicting that you will in the future.”<br>“I won’t lie to you. And about love? Unions have been built on far less than we have between us. We’d passion. Attraction. Respect.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <br>At the beginning, he is definitely not in love, but he is so persevering. I love the way as he treats Kaderin, and his unconditional support for her. He is a knight and a scholar in one person. I am amazed by his reasoning and discovery of tracing not only to a location but to a person as well. Oh, and I loved to read their scientific conversation on the plane after that hot night together.<br><br><b>Kaderin</b> is considered to be merciless and cold-hearted. She is the daughter of gods, a true warrior. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469620714i/19837676._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>She was so exquisite, and yet she carried a killer’s weapon. ... a sword not made for defense, not made for battle. The creature carried steel forged to deliver quick, silent deaths. Fascinating. An angel of death.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Sebastian makes her <i>feel</i> again, but Kaderin is obstinate and full of hate for vampires. She is often cruel and offensive to him, and it takes a while for her to accept him, to accept her own feelings for him. I understand her prejudices toward vampires, but I was so mad when she hurt that magnificent man. But at the end, in the pit of the Fyre Serpénte her trust in Sebastian was so touching, so I think I’m at peace with her after all. <br><br><b>
  <a href="http://exinasreadings.tumblr.com/tagged/No-Rest-for-the-Wicked" rel="nofollow noopener">My favorite quotes.</a>
</b></span>

<div id="review_23528446" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/23528446" />
    <a title="Auntee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/886675-auntee"><img alt="Auntee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1281897695p2/886675.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/23528446?book_show_action=true">Jun 02, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Auntee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Auntee" href="/user/show/886675-auntee">Auntee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Any romance fan, but especially fans of J.R. Ward</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Auntee by: </span>
      All my GR buddies--thank you!:)
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=keepers">keepers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer23528446" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2364012481774218327">What a fool I am! I've had this hot number sitting patiently in my TBR pile for months, just waiting for me to finally pick it up and read it! After reading the first two titles in the "Immortals After Dark" series, I was not in any real hurry to read further in the series. The first book was okay, and admittedly the second book was much better, but this one was just outstanding! I feel like I did when I finally got around to reading J.R. Ward's BDB. Now I can't wait to read more!<br/><br/>I'll admit I fe</span>
  <span id="freeText2364012481774218327" style="display:none">What a fool I am! I've had this hot number sitting patiently in my TBR pile for months, just waiting for me to finally pick it up and read it! After reading the first two titles in the "Immortals After Dark" series, I was not in any real hurry to read further in the series. The first book was okay, and admittedly the second book was much better, but this one was just outstanding! I feel like I did when I finally got around to reading J.R. Ward's BDB. Now I can't wait to read more!<br /><br />I'll admit I fell HARD for the hero in this book, the reluctant vampire named Sebastian Wroth. He was just the sweetest, sexiest guy, with all his vulnerabilities and his lacking in (sexual) self-confidence. And his "Bride", the valkyrie Kaderin the Cold Hearted--it took me a while to warm up to her. At first she was so mean and hurtful to Sebastian, I wondered why he stayed around. But then I grew to like her too, and by the end of the book I wanted her to get all that she dreamed of. I ended up loving these two as a couple!<br /><br />I loved the whole "Amazing Race-like" plot to the book. It was fast paced, and easier to follow than the previous books, maybe because it wasn't loaded down with a lot of 'lore' terms. And while the valkyries sometimes annoyed me in the previous books, this time I found their antics very amusing. I especially liked the reference to 'Survivor' host Jeff Probst--very funny!<br /><br />And although there weren't a lot of sex scenes, the few that were written were smokin' hot, and filled with emotion! Believe me, you won't even miss the lack of a lot of sex scenes, because the book is filled with longing, and sexual tension, and before you know it, it's almost over--and you won't want it to end! And if you're like me, you'll have tears in your eyes during the emotional final chapters.<br /><br />For all you sceptics who don't think you'd like a paranormal romance, give this one a try. I don't read many paranormals, but I loved this one! And for all you J.R. Ward fans--if you like the BDB books, but haven't found anything that could compare, I urge you to give this book a try. It completely captivated me.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2364012481774218327" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_73842382" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/73842382" />
    <a title="Dina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1918270-dina"><img alt="Dina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460302951p2/1918270.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/73842382?book_show_action=true">Oct 08, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dina" href="/user/show/1918270-dina">Dina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1918270-dina?shelf=series-immortals-after-dark">series-immortals-after-dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1918270-dina?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer73842382" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13505789437263177192">I guess third time <i>is</i> the charm... At least, with the <b>Immortals After Dark</b> series. I wasn't impressed with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6388558.The_Warlord_Wants_Forever__Immortals_After_Dark___1_' title='The Warlord Wants Forever (Immortals After Dark, #1) by Kresley Cole' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Warlord Wants Forever</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/14384.A_Hunger_Like_No_Other__Immortals_After_Dark___2_' title='A Hunger Like No Other (Immortals After Dark, #2) by Kresley Cole' rel='nofollow noopener'>A Hunger Like No Other</a>, the first two entries in the series, but now I understand what all the fuss is about. To be honest, I wasn't "feeling the love" in the first half of this book, but things got much better in the second half.<br/><br/>Back in 1709, Sebastian Wroth was turned into a vampire by his brother Nikolai, the hero in <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6388558.The_Warlord_Wants_Forever__Immortals_After_Dark___1_' title='The Warlord Wants Forever (Immortals After Dark, #1) by Kresley Cole' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Warlord Wants Forever</a>. That happened </span>
  <span id="freeText13505789437263177192" style="display:none">I guess third time <i>is</i> the charm... At least, with the <b>Immortals After Dark</b> series. I wasn't impressed with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6388558.The_Warlord_Wants_Forever__Immortals_After_Dark___1_" title="The Warlord Wants Forever (Immortals After Dark, #1) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">The Warlord Wants Forever</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/14384.A_Hunger_Like_No_Other__Immortals_After_Dark___2_" title="A Hunger Like No Other (Immortals After Dark, #2) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">A Hunger Like No Other</a>, the first two entries in the series, but now I understand what all the fuss is about. To be honest, I wasn't "feeling the love" in the first half of this book, but things got much better in the second half.<br /><br />Back in 1709, Sebastian Wroth was turned into a vampire by his brother Nikolai, the hero in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6388558.The_Warlord_Wants_Forever__Immortals_After_Dark___1_" title="The Warlord Wants Forever (Immortals After Dark, #1) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">The Warlord Wants Forever</a>. That happened against his will, and Sebastian has never forgiven his older brother for it. When Valkyrie Kaderin the Cold Hearted shows up at his castle to kill him, he's more than happy to oblige... until he realizes she's his Bride, the one and only female destined to be his eternal wife. Now he doesn't want to die anymore. Too bad Valkyries hate vampires and Kaderin is the best vampire slayer on the face of the Earth, er, the <i>Lore</i>.<br /><br />Kaderin isn't called "the Cold Hearted" for nothing. She hasn't felt any emotion in a thousand years, ever since her two sisters died by the hand of a vampire whose life Kaderin had just spared out of pity. Devastated by guilt and grief, she was given the <i>blessing</i> of feeling nothing so she could move on with her life. She's cold, fearless and ruthless, the ultimate vampire killer. But all that changes when she meets Sebastian and she starts feeling and experiencing emotions again. However, she isn't the least interested in consorting with a vampire, and she pushes him away.<br /><br />Besides, she needs to focus on the <i>Talisman's Hie</i>, which is basically an immortal version of the TV show <i>The Amazing Race</i>. Kaderin is the <i>Hie</i>'s reigning champion and has won every single edition of the deadly competition, so winning the <i>Hie</i> is a must. But there's more than pride and ego at stake this time around... This <i>Hie</i>, the winner will be given <i>Thrane's Key</i>, a powerful weapon that enables its possessor to time travel to the past. Here's Kaderin chance to go back in time and save her sisters! Her competitors are fierce, but she's positive she'll be able to defeat them. Sebastian offers to join her in the competition, but she flatly refuses his help. So he decides to enter the <i>Hie</i> himself and win the prize for her - after all, she's his Bride and he'll do anything for her. And while they're "globetrotting" in search of the talismans, he'll make her see they're meant for each other. Or will he?<br /><br />Awww, I loved, loved, loved Sebastian! How could I not? He was adorable, protective, caring, honorable, and sexy as hell. And I think he was a virgin! I loved how he got all nervous and tentative around Kaderin, before he realized she wasn't fragile like the women he knew in his previous human life. I have to say I didn't fully understand why he didn't end his own life in all the three hundred years he lived as an unwilling vampire before he met Kaderin and found a purpose to live, though. I guess I should believe it was <i>fate</i> and he was just waiting to meet her, but Kaderin's behavior didn't make it easy to go along with that idea because she was <i>so</i> not worthy of him... Not in the beginning, at least.<br /><br />I wanted to throttle Kaderin for the most part of this book. She was cold as expected, given her nickname, but I had a hard time figuring her out. I just couldn't understand how she remained imune to Sebastian for so long. At one point, she even lied to him and tried to use his feelings for her to get her out of a jammy so she could complete a task in the <i>Hie</i>. Thankfully, she came to her senses later in a wonderful scene that made my heart skip a beat. Was it enough to win me over? Not completely, but it was enough to stop me from wanting to smack her, LOL.<br /><br />The pace of the story was a bit uneven to me. I struggled to get through the first half, when Sebastian and Kaderin didn't really spend much time together and I couldn't see how they would manage to fall in love if they didn't get to know each other. Following the <i>Hie</i> was fun, but it wasn't enough to hold my interest for itself. Once Sebastian and Kaderin started to interact more often, things improved. The second half of the story had a nice mix of action and romance, and I would have read it in one sitting if it wasn't for the darn power outage that took my country by surprise last night. All in all, the final half of the story saved the book for me and the ending had a nice tease - not exactly a cliffhanger - that made me want to read the next book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/435045.Wicked_Deeds_on_a_Winter_s_Night__Immortals_After_Dark___4_" title="Wicked Deeds on a Winter's Night (Immortals After Dark, #4) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Wicked Deeds on a Winter's Night</a>. Yay!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13505789437263177192" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_35542627" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/35542627" />
    <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"><img alt=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1403239075p2/1570669.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/35542627?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="user" itemprop="url" name=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"> Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Lovers of heroes in pursuit, Vamp romance fans</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to  Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books) by: </span>
      2013 IAD Group reread
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=celibate-or-less-experienced-hero">celibate-or-less-experienced-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=favorite-or-autobuy-author">favorite-or-autobuy-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=warrior-woman">warrior-woman</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=desert-island-books">desert-island-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=owned-copy">owned-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=vampire">vampire</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=hero-to-die-for">hero-to-die-for</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=valkyrie">valkyrie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=dangerous-hero-challenge-2013">dangerous-hero-challenge-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer35542627" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12841118366325812297"><b>2nd Read Completed Between 8/11-8/12/13<br/><br/>There is something about this series that feels like sinking into a comfortable, well-loved pair of shoes, or diving into your favorite comfort dish (think Mac N' Cheese). These books absorb me like few others. I was excited to reread it, and hopeful I would feel more connected and like Kaderin more this time around. It actually happened, so yay!<br/><br/>Before, I felt like she was just so mean to Sebastian and it bothered me. This time, I could put her into context</b></span>
  <span id="freeText12841118366325812297" style="display:none"><b>2nd Read Completed Between 8/11-8/12/13<br /><br />There is something about this series that feels like sinking into a comfortable, well-loved pair of shoes, or diving into your favorite comfort dish (think Mac N' Cheese). These books absorb me like few others. I was excited to reread it, and hopeful I would feel more connected and like Kaderin more this time around. It actually happened, so yay!<br /><br />Before, I felt like she was just so mean to Sebastian and it bothered me. This time, I could put her into context of her life, and what she'd suffered. Her sorrow and her guilt at losing her sisters. How she couldn't bring them back, and had to live so many years without them. So she dedicated herself to wiping out those who had taken them from her. I could see why she was so armored against Sebastian. And yet, he found his way into her heart. That was a beautiful thing to experience, and it made me love Sebastian even more. I also realized that I did respect Kaderin. I think it's really easy to judge people for their mistakes and shortcomings (especially when we really don't know them). At church this Sunday, the pastor talked about the fact that people are 'holey' and we see all their holes and not the beauty of them as people. It was such a good message to remember. Sometimes, we are so 'holey' and those holes our own hurts cause us to become emotionally callous. As a result, we see others through jaundiced lens and just see what they do wrong, instead of how they are hurting as we hurt. This time around, I saw Kaderin for her pain, and what that pain made her do and act. The great thing about this story was that Sebastian loved her for who she was, and even when she pushed him away and hurt him, he didn't give up. That made me love him even more.<br /><br />I also saw Sebastian in a deeper and even more beloved way. I have much love for Sebastian. He's everything I would love in a man: a powerful warrior, equally powerful intellectual, thoughtful, caring, and loving! He's as deep as an ocean, and I find that so sexy. Absolutely sigh-worthy. I loved the scene when Sebastian was turned on by the highly intellectual discussion of time paradox with Kaderin, that she could hold her own. My kind of man. Nerdtastic--my Kryptonite! Like I said, Lachlain has some stiff competition!<br /><br />The concept of the Talisman's Hie was fun and exciting. I loved the globe-trotting adventure with a supernatural/fantastic twist. I liked the intense competition between Kaderin, Bowen, and Lucindeya. They all did some dirty tricks that made me wince. The Lore is so fantastically interesting, so learning more about it was fun. I felt bad for Bowen, even though I wanted Kaderin to win. I'm excited to see the sparks fly between Bowen and Mariketa. Of course, I love the interactions between Kaderin and her Valkyrie sisters, and Sebastian and his brother. It was great to see Nikolai and Myst (happy and together) so much in this book and to hear from Emma (and more obliquely Lachlain). As always, Cole has me laughing at the Valkyries' antics.<br /><br />Man, I love those Wroth brothers! *Thud* Times Four!<br /><br />It's exciting and lovely to see that I love these books just as much (if not more) the second time around.<br /><br />Check out my <a href="http://pinterest.com/gatadelafuente/immortals-after-dark-series-by-kresley-cole/" rel="nofollow noopener">Immortals After Dark Pinboard</a> on Pinterest!<br /><br />**Original Review Below***<br /><br />Another great book in the Immortals After Dark series. Can I be honest and say that I really disliked Kaderin at first? She is one valkryie with a Valhalla-sized chip on her shoulder (Bad pun, I know). I felt bad for how she had suffered, and normally I love a strong, kickbutt heroine. But she came off massively unsympathetic and heartless initially. I didn't like the way she treated Sebastian, who was the sweetest guy. I'd love a guy like him. But over time, I grew to like Kaderin as I came to understand why her heart was so cold. She had watched her three sisters get slaughtered by vampires, unable to do anything to save them. All she had left for over a millenia was a sworn oath to destroy all vampires. In her mind, they were all of the Horde, which are the vampires who have given over to Bloodlust. She didn't realize that there were good vampires who fought the Horde.<br /><br />Sebastian is a very loving character, but also a formidable warrior. He is one of the Wroth brothers, and was turned into a vampire by his oldest brothers Nikolai and Murdoch to fight in deposed Vampire King Kristoff's army to regain his kingdom. He was never good with women, being freakishly tall and lanky growing up. He had only been with two or three women in his life (compared to his playboy brother's Nikolai and Murdoch). He hated being a vampire, and was considering ending his miserable afterlife. But first he was going to try to win the Talisman Hie and get the Key, which would allow him to go back into the past and save his sisters who had died of plague back during the wars in their homeland Estonia. And then he sets his eyes on his Bride. Vampires are dead from the neck down, essentially. They cannot lust or feel desire for women until they meet their true Bride and become Blooded. It turns out that Kaderin the Coldhearted is Sebastian's Bride.<br /><br />He is in love and lust. He cannot think of anything other than wooing and having his bride. He follows her around like a lost puppy. For those readers who like the alpha male bad boys, that may not sound very appealing, but it really is. Sebastian is a delicious hero. His determination to win Kaderin was very appealing to me. Kaderin is pretty annoyed and vows to kill this annoying vampire, who keeps trying to protect her, and is helping her to win the Talisman's Hie. But soon, his attractive intensity, his warrior prowess, and his masculine appeal starts to melt the ice around her heart.<br /><br />So I started out this book holding Kaderin in dislike. However, seeing the way that Sebastian wins her over, and also how she is so tortured about the loss of her sisters, helped me to open my heart to Kaderin. She's not my favorite IAD heroine, but I do like her now. <br /><br />No Rest for the Wicked is a great follow up to A Hunger Like No Other. Although Kaderin's cold-hearted demeanor may not be to every reader's tastes, this book is a must read for fans of paranormal, especially vampire romances. It certainly opened my eyes to the appeal of a vampire lover.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="12841118366325812297" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5383610424577557224">HOW??? How does Kresley Cole do it??? This is PURE ENTERTAINMENT! I mean EVERY. SINGLE. BOOK. I can't even ... this series is so good that if you asked me to pick a favorite character, I simply can't. Everyone, and I mean EVERYONE, brings to the table that special something to make this series as entertaining and as fabulous as it is! I don't think I'll ever comprehend HOW some of these authors' imagination works. I find myself LOST in this magical world filled with these fascinating creatures t</span>
  <span id="freeText5383610424577557224" style="display:none">HOW??? How does Kresley Cole do it??? This is PURE ENTERTAINMENT! I mean EVERY. SINGLE. BOOK. I can't even ... this series is so good that if you asked me to pick a favorite character, I simply can't. Everyone, and I mean EVERYONE, brings to the table that special something to make this series as entertaining and as fabulous as it is! I don't think I'll ever comprehend HOW some of these authors' imagination works. I find myself LOST in this magical world filled with these fascinating creatures that Kresley created. HOW DOES ONE COME UP WITH ALL THESE THINGS?!?!?!? The names. The places. The things they battle. Not to mention the Hie!! And, of course, the sexy times ... when these guys get it on, sparks fly! And, in this case, I mean LITERALLY! LOVE LOVE LOVE everything about this series/author! As someone who's never gravitated towards fantasy/paranormal genre, I simply can't get enough of this series. Because, at the end of the day, a love story is a love story, right?? <br><br>Off I go onto book four ...<br><br>Cheers!<br><br><a href="http://amzn.to/2bhSCyN" rel="nofollow noopener">

      <a href="/user/show/3167458-anna-bobs-her-hair">Anna (Bobs Her Hair)</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1230196714" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16514616750290907469"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444922044i/16574279.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Fetish Cafe will be back in future installments. In the meantime, you can can get acquainted with the series in <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/367393428' rel='nofollow noopener'>Episode 1</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/260575073' rel='nofollow noopener'>Episode 2</a><br/><br/>Talk about a fun series! I didn't have any fetish boxes checked this time, but it's okay. I loved the read in spite of it. <br/><br/>I don't even mind that there's about a billion types of immortals in these books like I usually would (kitchen sink writing generally bugs me because it muddies the rules of a world/universe). This might have something to do with each race ha</span>
  <span id="freeText16514616750290907469" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444922044i/16574279.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Fetish Cafe will be back in future installments. In the meantime, you can can get acquainted with the series in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/367393428" rel="nofollow noopener">Episode 1</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/260575073" rel="nofollow noopener">Episode 2</a><br><br>Talk about a fun series! I didn't have any fetish boxes checked this time, but it's okay. I loved the read in spite of it. <br><br>I don't even mind that there's about a billion types of immortals in these books like I usually would (kitchen sink writing generally bugs me because it muddies the rules of a world/universe). This might have something to do with each race having their own set of quirks and problems. Kresley Cole handles her world with finesse, so it's all good. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Kaderin had never understood Myst's particular dislike of them. Now Kaderin knew Myst was right - they were a bunch of little hookers.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I don't even remember which race this was, but the rivalry between factions is hilarious. I probably wouldn't like nymphs or sirens either. <br><br>Kaderin and Sebastian were an unconventional couple. I'm not fully convinced that Sebastian could ever be a beta male. He was far too take-charge when he needed to be. But Kaderin was definitely the ALPHA female. There were no blushing, shy innocents in sight. And I'm a fan.<br><br>There was less romance and more story in this book than there were in the previous two books, but I don't think it hurt the couple at all. Seeing these two characters head-butt each other (literally) all over the world in a race to collect items in an immortal scavenger hunt was a bloody (again, literally) good time. <br><br>Thumbs up. On to the next book!</span>

    <a title="Jo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14323468-jo"><img alt="Jo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1434090906p2/14323468.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/450004532?book_show_action=true">Nov 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jo" href="/user/show/14323468-jo">Jo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14323468-jo?shelf=books-i-love">books-i-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14323468-jo?shelf=4-5-stars">4-5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14323468-jo?shelf=mine">mine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14323468-jo?shelf=heroines-i-love">heroines-i-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14323468-jo?shelf=book-boyfriend">book-boyfriend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14323468-jo?shelf=gr2017">gr2017</a>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer450004532" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8484614824811811714"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Sebastian was meant to call her his own. The good and the bad. She’d been made for him, and he for her. </b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <p>4.5stars - I loved this book!!</p> <blockquote>
  <i>There was a reason that would completely explain why she couldn’t hurt him. But she refused to entertain it—couldn’t. If she did, life as she knew it was over... </i>
</blockquote> <p>Strong heroines are a favorite of mine, and I just loved Kaderin the Cold Hearted. When she lost her beloved sisters’ centuries ago to a vampire attack, a gracious gift from an unknown </p></span>
  <span id="freeText8484614824811811714" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Sebastian was meant to call her his own. The good and the bad. She’d been made for him, and he for her. </b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <p>4.5stars - I loved this book!!</p> <blockquote>
  <i>There was a reason that would completely explain why she couldn’t hurt him. But she refused to entertain it—couldn’t. If she did, life as she knew it was over... </i>
</blockquote> <p>Strong heroines are a favorite of mine, and I just loved Kaderin the Cold Hearted. When she lost her beloved sisters’ centuries ago to a vampire attack, a gracious gift from an unknown source took her sorrow away, for which she was very grateful, but she also lost all emotion. Since then it’s been her goal to kill as many vampires as she can, until she meets Sebastian. A vampire whom she is unwilling to kill and who makes her feel for the first time since in millennia. I loved how vicious Kaderin was as a warrior, how good she was at kicking ass and taking names ;-) And her confusion and anger at falling for her enemy was very understandable, and I loved that despite all her hesitation, she just couldn’t ignore how he made her feel. </p> <blockquote>
  <i>Sebastian could give her something she wanted badly. He could win this competition, and in doing so, he could garner her affection.<br />In his mortal life, he’d been a knight but had no lady to offer his sword. Now he did.</i>
</blockquote> <p>I adored Sebastian and how different he was from the usual PNR heroes. He’s unsure of himself around women, a bit shy and a true gentleman. I loved that he believed in using his brain and his muscles when it came to fighting and the fact that he was a bit of a scholar – that was very sexy ;-) Since turned into a vampire against his will, Sebastian has been slowly losing himself, hoping to end the vampire life he despises, until he meets Kaderin, the valkyrie assassin meant to kill him, his Bride. I loved his immediate reaction to her, how fascinated he was and how determined he was to keep her. Of course I loved how possessive and protective he was over Kaderin, and how being with her eventually brought out the more confident and also ruthless side of him. </p> <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>For more than three hundred years, he’d waited for this.<br />And she was so fucking worth it. </b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <p>The romance was fantastic. I’m a big fan of instant attraction and I really liked how they author managed their fated romance. She made his body come to life and he made her feel, but it still took time for them to fall in love which felt more realistic. Sebastian determination to make Kaderin his was so very sexy and I loved that Kaderin couldn’t help but want Sebastian. The sexy times were scorching and I loved how passionate their romance was. </p> <blockquote>
  <i>The last time she’d seen her sisters had been when she’d buried them. To have a vision to replace that horror, she would do anything, eliminate anything that got in her way.</i>
</blockquote> <p>The plot was so excellent with the Talisman’s Hie, which is basically the equivalent of The Amazing Race, just very deadly and all the contestants are immortal. Kaderin has been the winner for the last few contests, but this year winning has become even more important – a chance to save her sisters. And with Sebastian determined to win her, entering the Hie so he could be with her, things got pretty heated between them. It was so exciting seeing the contestants travelling all over the world, seeking the relics which would gain them the most points. With Kaderin, Sebastian and Bowen MacRieve fighting by any means necessary to ensure they got the relics first, the plot was action-packed and very gripping. Especially knowing that Kaderin and Bowen had the most to lose if they lost – Kaderin with her chance to save her sisters and Bowen with his chance to save his mate who had died years ago. </p> <p>I love this series and all the various characters and fascinating world the author created. A definite must read for all PNR fans. </p></span>
  <a data-text-id="8484614824811811714" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
