<div id="review_130029211" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/130029211" />
    <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1352609417p2/2489554.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/130029211?book_show_action=true">Nov 09, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog">Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">paranormal romance fans, especially BDB fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=author-kresley-cole">author-kresley-cole</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-i-own">books-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-i-go-rabid-over">books-i-go-rabid-over</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=read-in-2011">read-in-2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=drinks-on-me">drinks-on-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=king-of-the-harem">king-of-the-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=my-hottie-harem">my-hottie-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=keep-a-spare-pair-of-knickers">keep-a-spare-pair-of-knickers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer130029211" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer346611773384407980"><b> re-read: April 2011</b><br/><br/>I have been rendered speechless. No Rest for the Wicked is so amazing, I don’t think any review I write can sum up its greatness. From the get-go, Cole sucks you right in! I couldn’t pace myself at all with this book. And although I tried to stop reading many times, I just couldn’t put the book down for more than twenty minutes. <br/><br/>First off, I just want to gush about how much I enjoyed the hero and heroine of this book. Sebastian Wroth was a human, who was unwilling turned into</span>
  <span id="freeText346611773384407980" style="display:none"><b> re-read: April 2011</b><br /><br />I have been rendered speechless. No Rest for the Wicked is so amazing, I don’t think any review I write can sum up its greatness. From the get-go, Cole sucks you right in! I couldn’t pace myself at all with this book. And although I tried to stop reading many times, I just couldn’t put the book down for more than twenty minutes. <br /><br />First off, I just want to gush about how much I enjoyed the hero and heroine of this book. Sebastian Wroth was a human, who was unwilling turned into a vampire by his brothers Nikolai and Murdoch. After the change, he lived a life of solitude alone and bitter until he found a reason to live again.<br /><br />Kaderin the Cold-Hearted is exactly that. She feels nothing and she considers the lack of emotions to be a blessing. Kaderin lost her two sisters in a battle against vampires. Unfortunately, the only vampire she spared slaughtered her sisters, Rika and Dasha right before her eyes. From that moment on, Kaderin dedicated her life to training and dealing death to the vampires that stole her sisters from her.<br /><br />But when Kaderin encounters a vampire that doesn’t fight against her killing blow, she spares him. But this time, the vampire doesn’t cause her heart to break yet again. Instead, he causes her to <i>feel</i>.<br /><br />I have to mention how adorable Sebastian is when his still heart beats for the first time in the presence of Kaderin. He thinks it’s an earthquake and fears the castle will crumble down on them. How adorable!<br /><br />I thought the relationship that Bastian and Kaderin shared was very believable. Kaderin is not about to fall hopelessly in love with a member of the race that she has killed ruthlessly for years. She is strong and independent and I think Cole makes their love develop at a reasonable pace. Even though Bastian recognizes her as his Bride, he admits that he doesn’t actually love her until they learn more of each other and trust each other. <br /><br />There is a lot of action in this book, thanks to the genius idea of The Hie, an immortal and dangerous version of The Amazing Race. The winner of the Hie is awarded Thane’s Key which every immortal would willingly die for. Kaderin is no exception, because the key allows two chances to travel back in time to change events. Kaderin will do anything to get her sisters back.<br /><br />As Kaderin competes, Bastian assists her in any way he can. And in their efforts, Kaderin learns to trust someone else with her feelings and Bastian learns that love is the one thing that is worth living for. <br /><br />Favourite Quote:<br />She was injured worse than he’d ever seen. The sand around her was dark. It was blood...everywhere.<br />“My God, why didn’t you say something?” he roared, furious again.<br />“Oh, pardon me for bleeding,” she muttered when she saw his eyes glued to her legs. Don’t want to whet your appetite.”<br />“You can be so coarse sometimes, wife.”<br />“Not your sodding wife.”<br />“<i>Yet</i>.”<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="346611773384407980" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer16925628511310558264">This definitely felt 2006-ish but i honestly didn’t have a problem with that. This is my 2nd book by Kresley Cole and i can say now that she’s an incredible writer— i’ll still reach for her books even if they’re meh. <br/>However, i must comment that her dialogues often feel comical and detached??? i really don’t know how else to put it but that’s pretty much how it felt. The <b>world building/setting</b> was a bit confusing, so i’ll be honest i schemed through a lot but that’s entirely on me as i skipped t</span>
  <span id="freeText16925628511310558264" style="display:none">This definitely felt 2006-ish but i honestly didn’t have a problem with that. This is my 2nd book by Kresley Cole and i can say now that she’s an incredible writer— i’ll still reach for her books even if they’re meh. <br />However, i must comment that her dialogues often feel comical and detached??? i really don’t know how else to put it but that’s pretty much how it felt. The <b>world building/setting</b> was a bit confusing, so i’ll be honest i schemed through a lot but that’s entirely on me as i skipped the first book. The ‘competition’ plot didn’t interest me at all i just wanted to read abt them both and plus the ending was also anticlimactic imo.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“His endless years at the castle, though he’d been alone and weary, had been a worthy sacrifice to have her.<br />Sebastian was meant to call her his own. The good and the bad. She’d been made for him, and he for her.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />I adored <b>Sebastian</b>—loving, shy, loyal, attentive, strong, smart and caring. <b>Kaderine</b>, feisty and sarcastically awesome. The <b>pining game</b> in here is no joke and not to forget it has the <i>
  <b>’Big guy Small girl trope’</b>
</i> (idk if that’s a thing but i dig it so hard these days)<br /><br />Anyways, i guess i’ll continue w this series since duh, it’s Kresley Cole.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“She crossed her arms over her chest, and his gaze landed on her damp cleavage. As he had that night on the coast, he looked like he was considering throwing her over his shoulder and tracing her back to his bed. “I do so wish my breasts would stop staring at your eyes.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b></span>

<div id="review_128076766" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/128076766" />
    <a title="Francesca the Fierce (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Francesca the Fierce (Under the Covers Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595947372p2/3108364.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/128076766?book_show_action=true">Oct 26, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Francesca the Fierce (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Francesca the Fierce (Under the Covers Book Blog)" href="/user/show/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog">Francesca the Fierce (Under the Covers Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781849834193" href="/book/show/10573596-no-rest-for-the-wicked">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=read-audio-books">read-audio-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=genre-paranormal-romance">genre-paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-read-2010">books-read-2010</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-read-2014">books-read-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-read-2019">books-read-2019</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer128076766" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8134780425697610266">Ahhh Sebastian! *swoons* He is the perfect man. Old-time gentleman, shy, knows what he wants and fights for it, just... perfect! I wish I had my own Sebastian!<br/><br/>OK, so now that I got that out of the way... Kaderin is a valkyrie and she's been "cursed" with not being able to feel for a thousand years, since the death of her sisters, who were killed by a vampire. She is tough (as all valkyrie are), loves and lives for killing vampires and for the Hie (like the Amazing Race). That whole concept was n</span>
  <span id="freeText8134780425697610266" style="display:none">Ahhh Sebastian! *swoons* He is the perfect man. Old-time gentleman, shy, knows what he wants and fights for it, just... perfect! I wish I had my own Sebastian!<br /><br />OK, so now that I got that out of the way... Kaderin is a valkyrie and she's been "cursed" with not being able to feel for a thousand years, since the death of her sisters, who were killed by a vampire. She is tough (as all valkyrie are), loves and lives for killing vampires and for the Hie (like the Amazing Race). That whole concept was new and interesting. Kaderin always enters (and wins) this race and this year is no different. Well, except for the fact that before it starts she hears of a vampire in a castle and goes there to slay him, but realizes that she can't. She is his Bride, and because of him, after so long, she starts to feel again. She in turn wakes him from years of misery.<br /><br />Sebastian is Nikolai Wroth's brother. He was turned by Nikolai against his will and has hated being a vampire during his whole existence. He just wishes for final death. And Kaderin is the one supposed to bring it to him, which he is fine with, until he realizes she's His. The one for him. His Bride. And he will do anything to have her, protect her, cherish her, and live eternity with her.<br /><br />While Kaderin has to compete in the Hie, Sebastian enters as well, with the intention of wining for her. The prize seems to be something she wants above all other things. A key to go back in time twice. He doesn't think it could work, and he doesn't know why she wants to get it, but he is determined to help her or win it for her. They have some competition, and some tough competition in the form of Bowen, the lykae who we met in the previous book, and who wants the key to go back in time and rescue his dead mate.<br /><br />There a lot of action, intrigue, and some pretty amazing sexual tension and eventually, yes, sex. And even though Sebastian is not a virgin, he's not the most experienced in that department so it's up to Kaderin to teach him, which he learns quickly, and to be his first in many things.<br /><br />Their relationship develops perfectly. It's not the "I'm in love" at first sight, their love develops from constantly being together, liking each other, their company, their support. Even though there were no major events in the overall world for this series, this was an excellent book and I'll be looking forward to reading the next one soon!</span>
  <a data-text-id="8134780425697610266" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1103480928" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1103480928" />
    <a title="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads"><img alt="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1396922701p2/4561998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1103480928?book_show_action=true">Nov 11, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" href="/user/show/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads">Carmel (Rabid Reads)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook " href="/book/show/13554428-no-rest-for-the-wicked">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Carmel (Rabid Reads) by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/2806016-melanie">Melanie</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads?shelf=audio">audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads?shelf=audio-2014">audio-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1103480928" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10846801809682281871"><b>Reviewed by: <a href='http://rabidreads.ca/2015/04/audiobook-review-no-rest-for-the-wicked-by-kresley-cole.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Rabid Reads</a>.</b><br/><br/>I’d originally intended to listen to one IMMORTALS AFTER DARK audiobook a month until I got caught-up on the series. Well, that plan flew the coop the moment Robert Petkoff began cooing in my ear. This installment was a step below its predecessor because other than Bowen, who was a secondary character, it came up short on werewolves, and was more story-centric than sextastic. At any rate, I found Kresley Cole’s version of the Amazing Race (Hie) to be quite ingenious; I t</span>
  <span id="freeText10846801809682281871" style="display:none"><b>Reviewed by: <a href="http://rabidreads.ca/2015/04/audiobook-review-no-rest-for-the-wicked-by-kresley-cole.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Rabid Reads</a>.</b><br /><br />I’d originally intended to listen to one IMMORTALS AFTER DARK audiobook a month until I got caught-up on the series. Well, that plan flew the coop the moment Robert Petkoff began cooing in my ear. This installment was a step below its predecessor because other than Bowen, who was a secondary character, it came up short on werewolves, and was more story-centric than sextastic. At any rate, I found Kresley Cole’s version of the Amazing Race (Hie) to be quite ingenious; I thought that the relationship between Sebastian &amp; Kaderin was better developed, and I liked the heroine more than Emmaline.<br /><br />The Lore’s attention shifted to vampires in NO REST FOR THE WICKED, and although the author didn’t forge a new path where this supe was concerned, I appreciated all of the little details that were conveyed. The one major difference between the Horde and Bastian made the couple’s romance possible, and the Blooded slant ensured that their on-the-spot connection was irrefutable. This novel also added another dimension to Tracing—a vamp’s ability to teleport to a known location—by having the protagonist be the first with the capacity to dial in to a person instead of a place, much to Kaderin’s frustration.<br /><br />The Hie didn’t just add a level of excitement to the story it also contributed to a challenging courtship. Sebastian used the race to woe his Bride by assisting competitors in exchange for precious information about his Valkyrie, and extorting sexual favours from Kaderin for points. I loved how the heroine proved worthy of her name at every turn by surprising the bloodsucker with her coldness and cunning. I mentioned in my review of book 1 that I dislike virgin immortals, so although this installment had one as well, it made me happy that it was Wroth instead of the stereotypical female.<br /><br />The narrator consistently outdoes himself with every IAD performance; I missed his Irish brogue, but was delighted that it still made brief appearances via a member of the MacRieve clan. And, I do believe Bowen’s tale is next—goody, goody gumdrops! Robert Petkoff’s female voices were remarkably good, and I couldn’t get over his energy during the romp sessions. I had my iPhone on speaker during one of them, and was thankful that I was home alone otherwise my husband would have thought that I’d started something without him. I’d have paid good money to be in the studio when he recorded that!<br /><br />NO REST FOR THE WICKED will light a fire in your belly; time to throw another Cole / Petkoff log on!</span>
  <a data-text-id="10846801809682281871" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1589756862" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1589756862" />
    <a title="Bubu" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44712859-bubu"><img alt="Bubu" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1510872559p2/44712859.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1589756862?book_show_action=true">Mar 24, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bubu" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bubu" href="/user/show/44712859-bubu">Bubu</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44712859-bubu?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44712859-bubu?shelf=1-star">1-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44712859-bubu?shelf=awful">awful</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1589756862" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5748385567672019534">There are not words enough to describe how much I disliked the heroine, Kaderin. At about 60% I considered going through the reviews I'd written and in which I had bashed the heroines to insert the following:<br/><br/><i>She's stupid, but not as stupid as Kaderin.<br/>She's annoying, but not as annoying as Kaderin.<br/>I disliked her, but not as much as Kaderin.<br/>etc...</i><br/><br/>She redefined <i>The Unlikable Heroine</i> for me. To call her TSTL would still give her wriggle room for positive attributes but she won't get that from me. No</span>
  <span id="freeText5748385567672019534" style="display:none">There are not words enough to describe how much I disliked the heroine, Kaderin. At about 60% I considered going through the reviews I'd written and in which I had bashed the heroines to insert the following:<br /><br /><i>She's stupid, but not as stupid as Kaderin.<br />She's annoying, but not as annoying as Kaderin.<br />I disliked her, but not as much as Kaderin.<br />etc...</i><br /><br />She redefined <i>The Unlikable Heroine</i> for me. To call her TSTL would still give her wriggle room for positive attributes but she won't get that from me. Not only is she stupid and annoying, Kaderin is infuriating, maddening, trying, tiresome, troublesome, ungrateful, undeserving, antagonistic and, worst of all, sexually manipulative. As Ally so nicely pointed it out in of my status updates for this book, Kaderin makes women look like manipulative idiots. To say her antagonistic antics drove me up the walls would require action from me, at least mentally. No, she stunned me into disbelief. I could plaster this review with those much beloved gifs to underline my feelings for her, but I'll refrain from doing so. She doesn't deserve it.<br /><br />Taking part in a Lore-based Treasure Hunt kind of thing which she has won for the past thousand years, she accuses two men of making it harder for her this time. Bowen, the hero of the next book, and her Soulmate Sebastian. This is the woman everybody fears - well - because she has won the Treasure Hunt for the past thousand years. Faced with new adversaries, Kaderin isn't doing as well as she used to. Blame the boys, Kaderin, blame the boys! How dare they participate? <br /><br />Sebastian who is blooded by her appearance in the first chapter of the book, thus marking her as his Bride, tries everything and anything to help her. Kaderin chooses to accept his help whenever it is convenient, meaning, when she has no chance of completing the assignment. So much for "I've been winning this for a millennium and I will never ever, ever, ever need your help. I'm a strong woman! How dare you even suggest I will need help? How patronising of you? How typically male? And I hate you because you're a Vampire, and I'll never be your Bride! What kind of a woman do you think I am?" Well, I hate to break it to you, Kaderin, you're the kind of woman who uses Sebastian's lust to manipulate him into helping you and you're okay with it. It'd be fine if you admitted it and took responsibility for your decisions. Your approach, however, makes you a hypocrite. That's who you are.<br /><br />Sebastian, on the other side, is the male version of a doormat. One-dimensional and lust driven to an extent that made me laugh. I understand the concept of Soulmates, that they can't help themselves, that it's Fate, Destiny, Kismet, whatever. All the more reason to make sure to create a well balanced couple because it's not as if any of these two could walk away from it, especially considering, since they're immortal, it'll be literally forever.<br /><br />There's so, so much more I could say here, point out all the weaknesses of Kaderin's character, and not even touch the ridiculous plot holes, but there's no point. I just wish I could give this book minus stars.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5748385567672019534" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText15435015329597614144" style="display:none">Story Rating 5 stars<br />Character Rating 5 stars<br />Romance Rating 4 stars<br />Imagination 5 stars<br />Heat Level 3.5 stars<br />Overall Rating 5 stars<br />Favorite Character, Sebastian<br /><br />I have a feeling that I'll be repeating this in every review I write on this series. I have to say again, Kresley Cole has written yet another FANTASTIC story filled with some of the best Imagination I've read to date. The characters are spectacular and along with the story just suck you in. I really enjoyed the aspects of this story with The Talisman's Hie.   <span id="freeText17621097074837574229" style="display:none">I really did hold out for a loooooonnnnnggggg time with this series.     <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2043222-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577660807p2/2043222.jpg" /></a>

<span id="freeTextContainer6744466881635476054">Revised Review:<br/>This is the third book in the series, and it follows <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/14384.A_Hunger_Like_No_Other__Immortals_After_Dark___2_' title='A Hunger Like No Other (Immortals After Dark, #2) by Kresley Cole' rel='nofollow noopener'>A Hunger Like No Other</a> very closely. The Talisman's Hie begins (sort of an immortal Amazing Race), and we see all of the scavenger hunt-like obstacles, we also see the set-up for the next book in the series <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/435045.Wicked_Deeds_on_a_Winter_s_Night__Immortals_After_Dark___4_' title='Wicked Deeds on a Winter's Night (Immortals After Dark, #4) by Kresley Cole' rel='nofollow noopener'>Wicked Deeds on a Winter's Night</a>. <br/>The Valkyrie Kaderin meets a vampire named Sebastian Wroth, brother of Nikolai Wroth from <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6388558.The_Warlord_Wants_Forever__Immortals_After_Dark___1_' title='The Warlord Wants Forever (Immortals After Dark, #1) by Kresley Cole' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Warlord Wants Forever</a>. Sebastian recognizes in her his Bride...the one he is destined to be with </span>
  <span id="freeText6744466881635476054" style="display:none">Revised Review:<br />This is the third book in the series, and it follows <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/14384.A_Hunger_Like_No_Other__Immortals_After_Dark___2_" title="A Hunger Like No Other (Immortals After Dark, #2) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">A Hunger Like No Other</a> very closely. The Talisman's Hie begins (sort of an immortal Amazing Race), and we see all of the scavenger hunt-like obstacles, we also see the set-up for the next book in the series <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/435045.Wicked_Deeds_on_a_Winter_s_Night__Immortals_After_Dark___4_" title="Wicked Deeds on a Winter's Night (Immortals After Dark, #4) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Wicked Deeds on a Winter's Night</a>. <br />The Valkyrie Kaderin meets a vampire named Sebastian Wroth, brother of Nikolai Wroth from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6388558.The_Warlord_Wants_Forever__Immortals_After_Dark___1_" title="The Warlord Wants Forever (Immortals After Dark, #1) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">The Warlord Wants Forever</a>. Sebastian recognizes in her his Bride...the one he is destined to be with for all eternity. She "bloods" him- he takes his first breaths, his heart beats, he gets his first erection...(eyebrow wiggle)<br />But she doesn't like vampires, she kills vampires, so he has his work cut out for him. <br /><br /><i>The Valkyrie covens were at war with the vampires even now, and the Lore was hurtling toward an Accession. During times like this, Kaderin was expected to be ridding vampires from the earth, not riding them." </i><br /><br />best quote from the book :D (thanks Annie)<br /><br />Sebastian enters the Hie to win the prize for Kaderin, but she is the reigning champ, so will she accept his help? or will she cut him out of the competition?<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6744466881635476054" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2540019639" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14320305171652303205">Exhilarating,Speedily page-turning and Sultry...in other words just again:WOW.<br/>Kresley Cole has surprised me yet AGAIN with "No Rest for the Wicked".!How the hell does she do it!!!?Keeping me awake the whole night reading this book once i started it and snarling towards anyone who might disturb me during the reading-i have it so bad(sigh). This book delivered it all for me,and like the others in the "Immortals After Dark"-series,i have completely fallen in love with this one, everything about it!</span>
  <span id="freeText14320305171652303205" style="display:none">Exhilarating,Speedily page-turning and Sultry...in other words just again:WOW.<br />Kresley Cole has surprised me yet AGAIN with "No Rest for the Wicked".!How the hell does she do it!!!?Keeping me awake the whole night reading this book once i started it and snarling towards anyone who might disturb me during the reading-i have it so bad(sigh). This book delivered it all for me,and like the others in the "Immortals After Dark"-series,i have completely fallen in love with this one, everything about it!<br /><br />I love it when Kresley Cole let her main-characters meet after one chapter into the story (or sometimes earlier than that,hehe) and having the valkyrie Kaderin the Cold-Hearted meet her mate in the youngest of the Wroth Brothers, vampire Sebastian Wroth. That meeting...GOD how it just BLEW me!!!!The tension and the stimulating sexual chemistry are OFF THE PAGES between these two,i love both of them individually and TOGETHER,these two...just stole my heart.!<br /><br />Kaderin is a character i so found intruging in the earlier books,and for her to have found her soulmate in Sebastian was fascinating for me-cuz i so wanted to know HOW.How he will steal this bruised heart...and my my Sebastan how you did it.Many sees Kaderin as a bitch who were mean to Sebastian,but in my opinion it was called for.She has after all lived with a cold unfeeling heart over a 1000 years and now joins a competition to win back her beloved sisters.Having met Sebastian and getting her emotions back was too heart-breaking for her, and not trusting him (and him also being a vampire,her enemy) she does everything to push him away..but the stubborn Sebastian refuses to let go of his Bride (vampires call their mates that) he joins the competition to win for her.<br /><br />Sebastian Wroth (be STILL my beating heart) is a Estonian hero that i will NEVER ever forget. God how Kresley Cole managed to keep him alive as a character, his emotions cutting through me. Just Wow.A soul hating the creature he is,he have been caging himself in Russia and lived out the next of his three centuries there. But once he finds his soulmate in Kaderin, he vows to make her his and never let her go. Like a lost puppy he always followed her everywhere throughout the journey, and i just WANTED TO EAT HIM UP!He protects her, fights for her,pleasures her,cares for her and he completely and utterly falls in love with her, wishing nothing but for her happiness. A man who was an excellent scholar and warrior in his mortal life have been very unlucky when it came to woman due to his high height which resulted to clumsyness at that time.(so he is very inexperienced)But as a blooded vampire and very obsessed with his Bride, jeezus what an Alpha he was! He was a very vulnerable man when it came to his feelings for Kaderin(he calls her Katja) but damn was he HOT AS FREAKING HELL when she pushed his buttons,and the love-scenes...YUMMI AND SO DELICIUS!Sebastian is very sexy in bed AND out of it.His intelligence, tender nature, possessiveness, the fight in him, and the powerful warrior inside him,yum!How he loves Kaderin for who she is and never giving up on her...and what he said in the end.Just GOD how i LOVE you Sebastian!Kiss kiss kiss!<br /><br />The mention about Regin`s reincarnated mate was exciting,she is one hell of a mad valkyrie,but damn i love her and i so look forward for her story.Meeting Emma and Lachlain again was delicius (even if it was just a phone call) they are as besotted as ever in each other!Big fat kiss from me to Nikolai and Myst,love these two so much!Now i look forward to Bowen and Mariketa`s story in the next book "Wicked Deeds on a Winter's Night",these two had some hot smoldering looks going on here..!<br /><br />Damn how i love this book. The Adventure, the chase, the prize...and with Sebastian and Kaderin falling in love during it all, just so amazing and equally sexy. I wish to find myself an Sebastian someday, and Kaderin just have to realize how damn lucky she is!(i know that she already has,hah).A Page-Turner and a favourite of mine now, thank you Kresley Cole,thank you for writing it!</span>
  <a data-text-id="14320305171652303205" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer126200872" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16097571181123336080">Now this is what I’m talkin’ about! Yes! Finally Kresley Cole decided to take this series one step further. After reading the previous two I was worried I’ll end up being blah towards this series, since I felt it was repetitive, but after this I think this will have a place among my favorites. The book had everything it needed: mind-blowing action, an amazing story, touching moments and hot love scenes. I’m really impressed.<br/><br/>Now, what I loved about the story was the dynamics of it. Yes, I prefer </span>
  <span id="freeText16097571181123336080" style="display:none">Now this is what I’m talkin’ about! Yes! Finally Kresley Cole decided to take this series one step further. After reading the previous two I was worried I’ll end up being blah towards this series, since I felt it was repetitive, but after this I think this will have a place among my favorites. The book had everything it needed: mind-blowing action, an amazing story, touching moments and hot love scenes. I’m really impressed.<br /><br />Now, what I loved about the story was the dynamics of it. Yes, I prefer something to catch my attention and keep it for at least 60% of the book. Unfortunately sometimes it’s difficult for me to find this. No Rest for the Wicked had my full attention from page one, even though I found that the beginning of the story was a bit too sudden. But it wasn’t so bad, eventually I managed to get used to this. The Amazing-Race-like competition was a very good idea; I guess this is what made the whole book so great.<br /><br />The characters were also nice. I am impressed with Sebastian, he can be a dualist at times and I find that interesting. He is such a kind and intelligent person. I must say I was expecting another brute, so this was a pleasant surprise for me. Kaderin… uhm… what can I say about her? I hated her. I really really did. I guess she wasn’t made for loving (except by poor Sebastian) so there was no surprise when I wanted to choke her to death. I actually got angry because the author exaggerated with Sebastian chasing her and kissing her ass so much. I doubt any man would do that even if she was his Bride. <br /><br />All in all I must say that this was a really great read. I can’t wait to see what the next one in this series is about.</span>

      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/6525208-no-rest-for-the-wicked">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=2019-read">2019-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=2014-read">2014-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer578909438" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3304415429204752078">June 2019 Re-read: Okay, so this book (and the next) are always especial favorites, because I love the Talisman's Hie. All the competition, and <i>Amazing Race-esque</i> action, just makes me ridiculously happy. Plus, though Sebastian and Kaderin do some questionable things to each other, like most HEA couples in this series, it's much less extreme here. <br/><br/>7 April 2015: <a href='http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B000MGATUI/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&camp=1789&creative=390957&creativeASIN=B000MGATUI&linkCode=as2&tag=touthenig-20&linkId=6JL5K62OAGZJE4ZA' rel='nofollow noopener'>$1.99 on Kindle</a><br/><br/>Book 1: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/122560174' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Warlord Wants Forever</a><br/>Book 2: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/578909308' rel='nofollow noopener'>A Hunger Like No Other</a><br/><br/>Here's the book that hooked me on this series. It had dept</span>
  <span id="freeText3304415429204752078" style="display:none">June 2019 Re-read: Okay, so this book (and the next) are always especial favorites, because I love the Talisman's Hie. All the competition, and <i>Amazing Race-esque</i> action, just makes me ridiculously happy. Plus, though Sebastian and Kaderin do some questionable things to each other, like most HEA couples in this series, it's much less extreme here. <br /><br />7 April 2015: <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B000MGATUI/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=390957&amp;creativeASIN=B000MGATUI&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;tag=touthenig-20&amp;linkId=6JL5K62OAGZJE4ZA" rel="nofollow noopener">$1.99 on Kindle</a><br /><br />Book 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/122560174" rel="nofollow noopener">The Warlord Wants Forever</a><br />Book 2: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/578909308" rel="nofollow noopener">A Hunger Like No Other</a><br /><br />Here's the book that hooked me on this series. It had depth that the novella, <i>The Warlord Wants Forever</i> necessarily lacked and the characters are FANTASTIC - without any of the 'coming into her own' of the heroine like in <i>A Hunger Like No Other</i>. It also included everything I love about the world, and as an added bonus: the Talisman's Hie - an <i>Amazing Race</i> type event, on supernatural steroids.<br /><br />Kaderin hasn't felt a thing, not the sorrow that was tearing her apart, not joy, hate, love, regret...nothing, for nearly a thousand years. After she lost her sisters blood sisters (triplets they were) her emotions were shut off. She never felt the lack, she simply dedicated herself to eradicating vampires. I loved Kaderin. She wasn't sure about anything when her feelings started coming back, not sure exactly how to deal with the onslaught (and I loved how it was initially shown to return) of emotions racing through her. But her personality shines through. Kaderin kicks ass, first, second, and third. But she's also got this beautiful understanding and kindness and compassion that shows through. She sees the beauty in, what others would deem, ugly and dangerous things - showing that she knows there's reason and right for everything to exist and thrive. All of that doesn't mean that she is willing to sacrifice herself for someone not completely and utterly <i>hers</i>, but she will give everything in her for one she loves.<br /><br />Bastian, and I just have to say how much I love that name, it's one of my favorites, is my favorite type of hero. He's intelligent - a scholar in his human life - and mostly <i>beta</i>. He wants to <b>woo</b> his <i>Katya</i>, winning her heart and having her want him for himself. He's not terribly experienced in relationships, and is a bit shy - at first. I love, love, love that even though Bastian desperately wants to push further with Kaderin he respects women too much to do so. He won't go where he's not wanted, and Kaderin keeps pushing him away. So he continues trying to bargain with her, and coax her to him. His <i>leverage</i> may not always be strictly gentlemanly, but I love that he knows when to push and when to back off. I also really, really love that - despite there being lust and 'fated mates' between them - Kaderin and Bastian admit several times throughout the novel that it isn't <b>love</b>...yet. <br /><br />Watching them fall in love is an immensely satisfying, joyous thing. <br /><br />I've already talked, probably at length, about the world in which this takes place. I'll only continue to reiterate that it's one of the most detailed, complex, in-depth worlds I've ever encountered. Kresley Cole continues to blow my mind with the way she weaves in multiple storylines and keep track of a labyrinthine time-line.<br /><br />The secondary characters are all interesting - I want to know ALL their stories. I won't even list them all here because there's too many. Fortunately it seems like Cole is in no hurry to stop writing in this series, and as I continue to love them, and the stakes continue to raise, I can't be more grateful.<br /><br />One of the new things in this novel is the Talisman's Hie. A race for immortals around the world to retrieve difficult objects of different power. All to gain points to be able to go for the final round. I loved this. I can't even explain how much. The competition, the characters competing against - and sometimes helping - each other, and the different locations it takes us to.<br /><br />Next up: <i>Wicked Deeds on a Winter's Night</i>. I'm so excited to read about Bowen again!</span>
  <a data-text-id="3304415429204752078" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mel" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mel" href="/user/show/2295424-mel">Mel</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2295424-mel?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer66128939" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7073301742504716882">If you like romance, sizzling moments and lots of humor, you're good with the Immortal After Dark series. <br/>In this third installment we see what happens when reluctant vampire Sebastian Wroth discovers that Valkyrie vampire-assassin Kaderin the Cold Hearted is his fated Bride. <br/><br/>This story was exciting, fun and sexy. <br/>Sebastian was a total sweetheart. Meeting Kaderin makes his miserable vampire existence finally meaningful and he goes out of his way to win her over. And she is one tough cookie...<br/>Wha</span>
  <span id="freeText7073301742504716882" style="display:none">If you like romance, sizzling moments and lots of humor, you're good with the Immortal After Dark series. <br />In this third installment we see what happens when reluctant vampire Sebastian Wroth discovers that Valkyrie vampire-assassin Kaderin the Cold Hearted is his fated Bride. <br /><br />This story was exciting, fun and sexy. <br />Sebastian was a total sweetheart. Meeting Kaderin makes his miserable vampire existence finally meaningful and he goes out of his way to win her over. And she is one tough cookie...<br />What I liked most was that the instant attraction between the hero and heroine wasn't confused with love. It slowly evolves through out the book and both Sebastian and Kaderin have their own demons to battle before falling into each other's arms.<br /> <br />I loved the Valkyries. I'm sure I'll be talking in their words when I say: those are some crazy bitches! Especially Regin and nucking futs Nïx cracked me up and I can't wait to read their books. <br /><br />I might be one of very few but I think I liked #2 of Immortals After Dark <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/14384.A_Hunger_Like_No_Other__Immortals_After_Dark___2_" title="A Hunger Like No Other (Immortals After Dark, #2) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">A Hunger like no Other</a> even more than this one... <br />Sebastian (cool and strong but sweet and considerate) couldn't be farther apart from Lachlain (out of his mind, forceful -in the beginning- and overbearing) but to me, Lachlain brought a bit more intensity to the table. <br />Of course, this only shows that in fantasy we choose our heroes waaaay differently then we would in real life...</span>

There was just something that felt like it took forever!<br/><br/>I totally loved Sebastian though. Loved him.<br/><br/>I do have to admit that a lot of my focus was spent on Bowen. I am beside myself in horror over what he went through in this book. Appalled even. My heart aches for him. <br/><br/>Yeah, his book is next.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('X3oVxiGG7oKEbTv2uJrljdnblORpSZ12rvmpnzrdDTtrp1TqODPqU+KShyF8tXTpgUEt5ccUSnSNtryMCJR6Kg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ok5mRsM5SzFW8YhpkXIM0fFGZwkSSflTsXaIeCTrS++Wkydq2oxP4DAONL5VXZ21qdzeCLwULlGSOZ1rFqI8/g==')})
  }

  <span id="freeText600593607176548762" style="display:none">Kresley Cole is the #1 <i>New York Times</i> bestselling author of the electrifying Immortals After Dark paranormal series, the young adult Arcana Chronicles series, the erotic Gamemakers series, and five award-winning historical romances.<br /><br />A master’s grad and former athlete, she has traveled over much of the world and draws from those experiences to create her memorable characters and settings. <br />Her IAD books have been translated into 23 foreign languages, garnered three RITA awards, a RWA Hall of Fame induction, and consistently appear on the bestseller lists, in the U.S. and abroad.<br /><br />Cole lives in Florida with her family. Learn more about Kresley at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.kresleycole.com">www.kresleycole.com</a> &amp; <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.thearcanachronicles.com">www.thearcanachronicles.com</a><br /><br /></span>
